The following actions are running on Node.js 20 and may not work as expected: actions/checkout@v4, actions/github-script@v7, dorny/paths-filter@v3. Actions will be forced to run with Node.js 24 by default starting June 2nd, 2026. Node.js 20 will be removed from the runner on September 16th, 2026.
